2518 <div class="Page-body ArticlePage-articleBody" itemprop="articleBody">

2519<div class="RichTextArticleBody">

2520

2521

2522 <div class="RichTextArticleBody-body">

2523<p>

2524The Fox 13 Dream Team is on a mission to change lives.</p>

2525

2526<p>

2527We’ve partnered with Mountain America Credit Union, Woodside Homes and Smith’s Food and Drug to help honor some deserving Utahns.</p>

2528

2529<p>

2530This month, the Dream Team surprised Percy Pearson.</p>

2531

2532<p>

2533Percy is the President of the Rose Park Sports Association and coaches the Rose Park Panthers Youth Travel football team.</p>

2534

2535<p>

2536The team is made up of boys between the ages of 10 and 14.</p>

2537

2538<p>

2539Coach Pearson goes to great lengths to make sure any kid who wants to play has an opportunity to do so. As a result, he’s reached into his own pocket many times to cover the costs of program fees and uniforms for kids from single parent families, children in Foster Care, and children who are homeless.</p>

2540

2541<p>

2542Watch the video to see how the Dream Team surprised the Panthers during one of their practices.</p>

2543

2544<p>

2545If you know someone who could use a visit from the Dream Team, <a class="Link" href="https://fox13now.com/2018/02/23/nominate-a-deserving-person-or-family-for-a-visit-from-the-fox-13-dream-team/" target="_blank">

2546fill out the nomination form here.</a>

2547 Tell us the story of the person you are nominating, as it might be told on TV, and suggest a gift that could make a difference in their life.</p>

2548
